                <script type="text/javascript">
                 mdc.module.setModule({
    name: 'SEARCH_COMPONENT__213857412',
    mdi: {
      name: mdc.module.getMdiModuleName()
    },
    function: function (self, api) {
      var $content = api.getModuleNode();
      var $element = $content.select('[name="trdDd"]');

      
      var params = {
        baseName: 'krx.mdc.i18n.component',
        key: 'B128.bld',
        locale: 'ko'
      };

      var queryString = 'null';
      if (queryString && queryString !== 'null') {
        var queryArray = queryString.split('&');
        queryArray.forEach(function (query) {
          var name = query.split('=')[0];
          var value = query.split('=')[1] || '';
          params[name] = value;
        });
      }
      

      
        
          var calendarOption = {};
          var input = [];
          
            
              
              input.push($content.select('[name="trdDd"]'));
              
            
          

          
          var date = '';
          api.util.submitAjax({
            method: 'GET',
            url: '/comm/bldAttendant/executeForResourceBundle.cmd',
            async: false,
            data: params,
            success: function (data) {
              var output = data['result']['output'];
              output.forEach(function (item) {
                $.each(item, function (key, value) {
                  date = value;
                });
              });
            }
          });

          if (date) {
            input.forEach(function (item) {
              item.val(date);
            });

            //=== (20201028, 김정삼) compIdDateLimit 값을 지정한 경우 이 지정값(bld)으로 달력팝업활성화 종료일 기준을 변경한다
            
            calendarOption.limit = date;

            var compIdDateLimit = 'B128';
            var compId = 'B128';
            if (compIdDateLimit && compIdDateLimit !== compId) {
              api.util.submitAjax({
                method: 'GET',
                url: '/comm/bldAttendant/executeForResourceBundle.cmd',
                async: false,
                data: $.extend(params, {key: compIdDateLimit + '.bld'}),
                success: function (data) {
                  var output = data['result']['output'];
                  output.forEach(function (item) {
                    $.each(item, function (key, value) {
                      calendarOption.limit = value;
                    });
                  });
                }
              });
            }
            
            //===/

            //=== (20201215, 김상훈) restictId 값을 지정한 경우 이 지정값(bld)으로 조회가능 시작일을 제한한다.
            
            var restictId = 'B155';
            var menuId = mdc.getMdiView() ? mdc.getMdiView().id : '';

            if (restictId && (menuId !== '' && menuId !== undefined)) {
              params['menuId'] = menuId;
              api.util.submitAjax({
                method: 'GET',
                url: '/comm/bldAttendant/executeForResourceBundle.cmd',
                async: false,
                data: $.extend(params, {key: restictId + '.bld'}),
                success: function (data) {
                  var output = data['result']['output'];
                  calendarOption.restrictDate = output[0]['restrict_date'];
                }
              });
            }
            
            //===/

            

          }
          

          calendarOption.input = input;
          calendarOption.positionTop = false;
          calendarOption.showButton = true;
          calendarOption.disabledDate = 'null';
          calendarOption.disabledTp = 'null';
          calendarOption.changeStrtDate = 'false';
          calendarOption.validatePeriodBusDate = 'B161';
          $.fn.calendar(calendarOption);
        

        
      

      

      
    }
  });
                </script>

                </a>

        });
      

      
    }
  });
                </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         mdc.module.setModule({
    name: 'MDCSTAT015_0',
    init: 'init',
    mdi: {
      name: mdc.module.getMdiModuleName(),
      event: {
        afterViewActivated: ['resizeGrid'],
        afterViewSizeChanged: ['resizeGrid']
      }
    },
    function: function (self, api) {
      var $content = api.getModuleNode();
      var $f = $content.select('#MDCSTAT015_FORM');

      self.resizeGrid = function (e) {
        self.grid.setHeight(e.getContentLeftHeight());
        self.grid.resize();
      };

      self.init = function () {
        self.grid = api.util.grid.init({
          node: api.getModuleNode().getNode(),
          form: $f,
          layout: 'no-apply',
          grid: [
            {
              template: $content.select('#jsGrid_MDCSTAT015_0'),
              bld: 'dbms/MDC/STAT/standard/MDCSTAT01501',
              bldDataKey: 'OutBlock_1',
              unit: {
                share: ['ACC_TRDVOL', 'LIST_SHRS'],
                money: ['ACC_TRDVAL', 'MKTCAP']
              },
              fluctuation: {
                reference: 'FLUC_TP_CD',
                column: [
                  {
                    name: 'CMPPREVDD_PRC',
                    useArrow: true
                  },
                  {
                    name: 'FLUC_RT'
                  }
                ]
              }
            }
          ]
        });

        self.getList();
      };

      self.getList = function () {
        var mktId = $content.select('input[name="mktId"]:checked').val();
        if ( mktId === 'ALL' ) {
          self.grid.hideColumns(0, []);
        } else if (mktId === 'STK') {
          self.grid.hideColumns(0, ['MKT_NM', 'SECT_TP_NM']);
        } else {
          self.grid.hideColumns(0, ['MKT_NM']);
        }

        self.grid.appendRow(); // 설정한 form 과 bld 를 바탕으로 서비스 조회 후 그리드에 데이터 삽입
      }
    }
  });
        </script>

        <script type="text/javascript">
         mdc.module.setModule({
    name: 'MDCSTAT019_1',
    init: 'init',
    mdi: {
      name: mdc.module.getMdiModuleName(),
      event: {
        afterViewActivated: ['resizeGrid'],
        afterViewSizeChanged: ['resizeGrid']
      }
    },
    function: function (self, api) {
      var $content = api.getModuleNode();
      var $f = $content.select('#MDCSTAT019_FORM');

      self.resizeGrid = function (e) {
        self.grid.setHeight(e.getContentLeftHeight());
        self.grid.resize();
      };

      self.init = function () {
        self.grid = api.util.grid.init({
          node: api.getModuleNode().getNode(),
          form: $f,
          layout: 'no-apply',
          grid: [
            {
              template: $content.select('#jsGrid_MDCSTAT019_0'),
              bld: 'dbms/MDC/STAT/standard/MDCSTAT01901',
              bldDataKey: 'OutBlock_1',
              unit: {
                share: ['LIST_SHRS']
              }
            }
          ]
        });

        self.getList();
      };

      self.getList = function () {
        self.grid.appendRow(); // 설정한 form 과 bld 를 바탕으로 서비스 조회 후 그리드에 데이터 삽입
      }
    }
  });
        </script>

     <script type="text/javascript">
      mdc.module.setModule({
    name: 'MDI_MODULE',
    init: 'init',
    mdi: {
      isMdiModule: true
    },
    function: function (self, api) {

      var $searchResultWrap = $('#jsMdiSearchResultWrap');
      var $menuSearchValue = $('#jsMdiMenuSearchValue');
      var menuSearch = new api.util.MenuSearch('mdi', 1000);

      self.init = function () {
        // mdi 모듈 객체 로드
        self.mdi = api.getMdi();
        // mdi 모듈 초기화
        self.mdi.init($('.content'), $('#jsMdiMenu'), $('#jsMdiTab'), $('#jsMdiContent'));
        var params = {
          
          
          'menuId':'MDC0201020101',
          
          
        };
        if (params['menuId']) {
          self.mdi.openView(params['menuId'], params);
        }
      };

      // 메뉴검색
      var searchMenuList = function (value) {
        value = value.trim();
        var menus = menuSearch.searchMenu(value);
        if (menus.length > 0) {
          var menuName;
          var screenId;
          var screenNo;
          var menuPath;
          menus.forEach(function (menu) {
            menuName = menu['MENU_NM'] || '';
            screenId = menu['SCREN_ID'] || '';
            screenNo = menu['SCREN_NO'] || '';
            menuPath = menu['MENU_PATH'] ? menu['MENU_PATH'].replace(/>/gi, '<em>&gt;</em>') : '';
            $searchResultWrap.append($('<LI>').attr('data-menu-id', menu['MENU_ID']).append($('<SPAN>').append(screenNo)).append(menuPath)/*.append($('<DFN>')).append(menuName)*/);
          });
        } else {
          $searchResultWrap.append($('<LI>').text(mdc.lang.getMessage('MG027'))); //검색결과가 존재하지 않습니다.
        }

        $searchResultWrap.closest('div').show();
      };

      var getMenuIdByValue = function (value) {
        value = value.trim();
        var menu = menuSearch.searchCoincidentMenu(value) || {};
        return menu['MENU_ID'];
      };

      var openView = function (menuId) {
        self.mdi.openView(menuId);
        $menuSearchValue.val('');
        $searchResultWrap.closest('div').hide();
        $searchResultWrap.empty();
      };

      $menuSearchValue.on('keyup', _.debounce(function (e) {
        console.log(e.keyCode);
        // 엔터, ESC, 방향키
        if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 27 || (e.keyCode >= 37 && e.keyCode <= 40)) {
          e.preventDefault();
          return;
        }

        var value = this.value;
        $searchResultWrap.empty();
        if (value.length > 0) {
          searchMenuList(value);
        } else {
          $searchResultWrap.closest('div').hide();
        }
      }, 500));

      $menuSearchValue.on('keydown', function (e) {
        var $li;
        var $liOn;
        if (e.keyCode === 13 || e.keyCode === 38 || e.keyCode === 40) {
          e.preventDefault();
          $li = $searchResultWrap.find('li[data-menu-id]');
          $liOn = $searchResultWrap.find('li.on[data-menu-id]');
        }

        // 엔터
        if (e.keyCode === 13) {
          if ($liOn.length > 0) {
            openView($liOn.data('menu-id'));
          } else {
            $('#jsMdiMenuSearchButton').click();
          }
        }

        // ESC
        if (e.keyCode === 27) {
          $searchResultWrap.closest('div').hide();
        }

        // 방향키 위
        if (e.keyCode === 38) {
          if ($liOn.length > 0) {
            if ($liOn.eq(0).prev().length) {
              $liOn.eq(0).removeClass('on');
              $liOn.eq(0).prev().addClass('on');
              $liOn.eq(0).prev()[0].scrollIntoView(false);
            }
          }
        }

        // 방향키 아래
        if (e.keyCode === 40) {
          if ($li.length > 0) {
            if ($liOn.length > 0) {
              if ($liOn.eq(0).next().length > 0) {
                $liOn.eq(0).removeClass('on');
                $liOn.eq(0).next().addClass('on');
                $liOn.eq(0).next()[0].scrollIntoView(false);
              }
            } else {
              $li.eq(0).addClass('on');
            }
          }
        }
      });

      $(document).on('click', function (e) {
        var $target = $(e.target);
        if ($target.closest('.lnb_search').length === 0 && $target.closest('.lnb_searched').length === 0) {
          $searchResultWrap.closest('div').hide();
        }
      });

      $('#jsMdiMenuSearchButton').on('click', function () {
        var value = $menuSearchValue.val().trim();
        if (!value) {
          alert(mdc.lang.getMessage('MG026')); //검색어를 입력하세요.
          return;
        }

        value = getMenuIdByValue(value);
        if (!value) {
          alert(mdc.lang.getMessage('MO045')); //일치하는 메뉴가 없습니다.
          return;
        }

        openView(value);
      });

      $searchResultWrap.on('click', 'li[data-menu-id]', function () {
        openView($(this).data('menu-id'));
      });

      // 전체 탭 닫기 이벤트
      $('#jsCloseAllViewsButton').on('click', function () {
        self.mdi.closeAllViews();
        /*
        if ($('#jsViewSizeButton').hasClass('size_max')) {
          $('#jsViewSizeButton').click();
        }
        */
      });

      // MDI 확대/축소 이벤트
      $('#jsViewSizeButton').on('click', function () {
        if ($('#jsViewSizeButton').hasClass('size_max')) {
          $('.btn_content_size_btn').removeClass('size_max');
          $('.btn_lnb').removeClass('size_max');
          $('.container').removeClass('size_max');
          if($('#jsMdiMenuButton').hasClass('hide')){
            $('.content').css('width', 'calc(100% - 40px)');
          }else{
            $('.content').css('width', 'calc(100% - 240px)');
          }
          if (ci.agent.isIe === true) {
            $('.bottomround').css('width', '200px');
          }
          $('.header').show();
          self.mdi.contractView();
        } else {
          $('.btn_content_size_btn').addClass('size_max');
          $('.btn_lnb').addClass('size_max');
          $('.container').addClass('size_max');
          if ($('#jsMdiMenuButton').hasClass('hide')) {
            $('.content').css('width', 'calc(100% - 40px)');
          } else {
            $('.content').css('width', 'calc(100% - 240px)');
          }
          if (ci.agent.isIe === true) {
            $('.bottomround').css('width', '200px');
          }
          $('.header').hide();
          self.mdi.expandView();
        }
      });

      $('#jsMdiTabListButton').on('click', function () {
        var $tabList = $('.CI-MDI-TAB-LIST');
        if (!$tabList.hasClass('active')) {
          $tabList.find('ul').empty();
          var views = self.mdi.getViews();
          views.forEach(function (view) {
            self.mdi.appendTabList(view);
          });
        }
        $tabList.toggleClass('active');
      });

      $('.CI-MDI-TAB-LIST').on('click', 'a', function () {
        var menuId = $(this).closest('li').attr('data-menu-id');
        self.mdi.openView(menuId);
      });

      $('.CI-MDI-TAB-LIST').on('click', 'button', function () {
        var menuId = $(this).closest('li').attr('data-menu-id');
        self.mdi.closeView(menuId);
      });

      // 메뉴 열기/닫기 이벤트
      $('#jsMdiMenuButton').on('click', function () {
        var containerWidth = $('.container').width();
        if ($('#jsMdiMenuButton').hasClass('hide')) {
          $('.btn_lnb').removeClass('hide');
          $('.content').removeClass('size_max');
          $('.lnb > .lnb_search, .lnb > .lnb_tree').animate({left:0}, 500);
          $('.btn_lnb').animate({left:200}, 500);
          $('.lnb').animate({width:200}, 500);
          $('.bottomround').show();
          $('.content').animate({width: containerWidth - 240}, 500, function () {
            $(this).css('width', 'calc(100% - 240px)');
            self.mdi.showMenu();
          });
        } else {
          $('.btn_lnb').addClass('hide');
          $('.content').addClass('size_max');
          $('.lnb > .lnb_search, .lnb > .lnb_tree').animate({left:-200}, 500);
          $('.btn_lnb').animate({left:0}, 500);
          $('.lnb').animate({width:0}, 500);
          setTimeout(function () {
            $('.bottomround').hide();
          }, 500);
          $('.content').animate({width: containerWidth - 40}, 500, function () {
            $(this).css('width', 'calc(100% - 40px)');
            self.mdi.hideMenu();
          });
        }
      });

      // 검색조건 및 footer 열기 / 닫기
      $('#jsMdiContent').on('click', '.CI-MDI-COMPONENT-BUTTON', function () {
        var $this = $(this);
        var $div = $this.siblings('div');
        if ($div.is(':visible')) {
          $div.hide();
          if ($div.data('component') === 'search') {
            $this.addClass('on2');
            $this.text('Open');
          } else {
            $this.closest('.CI-MDI-COMPONENT-FOOTER').addClass('on2');
            $this.text('Open');
          }
        } else {
          $div.show();
          if ($div.data('component') === 'search') {
            $this.removeClass('on2');
            $this.text('Close');
          } else {
            $this.closest('.CI-MDI-COMPONENT-FOOTER').removeClass('on2');
            $this.text('Close');
          }
        }

        if ($div.data('component') === 'search') {
          self.mdi.triggerModuleEvent();
        }
      });

      // 브라우저 리사이징 이벤트
      api.util.addEvent(window, 'resize', _.debounce(function () {
        self.mdi.triggerModuleEvent();
      }, 500));

    }
  });
     </script>
     <!--b:e-->
    </section>
    <!-- //CONTENT -->
   </section>
   <!-- //CONTAINER -->

  <script type="text/javascript">
   mdc.module.setModule({
			name: 'TEMPLET_MODULE',
			init: 'init',
			function: function (self, api) {

				var SESSION_TIMEOUT = 30;

				self.init = function () {
					if("en"==""){
						mdc.util.setCookie("lang","en",365);					
					}else if("ko_KR"==""){
						mdc.util.setCookie("lang","ko_KR",365);
					}
					if ($('#jsLogoutBtn').length > 0) {
						timeoutForLogout();
					}
				};

				var makeDigitNumber = function (number) {
					var digitNumber = number + '';
					if (number < 10) {
						digitNumber = '0' + number;
					}
					return digitNumber;
				};

				var confirmForLogout = function () {
					api.util.submitAjax({
						url: '/contents/MDC/MAIN/main/removeSession.cmd',
						success: function () {
							api.layer.confirm('세션 만료로 자동 로그아웃 되었습니다.<br><span style="font-weight:600;">서비스 이용을 위해 재로그인 해주세요.</span>', function () {
								location.href = '/contents/MDC/COMS/client/MDCCOMS001.cmd';
							}, function () {
								location.href = '/contents/MDC/MAIN/main/index.cmd';
							});
						}
					});
				};

				var timeoutForLogout = function () {
					if (self.timeoutForLogout) {
						clearInterval(self.timeoutForLogout);
					}
					var date = new Date();
					date.setMinutes(date.getMinutes() + SESSION_TIMEOUT);
					document.cookie = 'mdc.client_session=' + encodeURIComponent('true') + '; path=/; expires=' + date.toUTCString() + ';';
					var minute = SESSION_TIMEOUT;
					var second = 0;
					self.timeoutForLogout = setInterval(function () {
						second -= 1;
						if (second < 0) {
							minute -= 1;
							second = 59;
						}
						if (minute < 0 || api.util.getCookie('mdc.client_session') !== 'true') {
							minute = 0;
							second = 0;
							confirmForLogout();
							clearInterval(self.timeoutForLogout);
						}
						$('#jsLogoutTime').text(makeDigitNumber(minute) + '분 ' + makeDigitNumber(second) + '초');
					}, 1000);
				};

				$('#jsExtendLoginBtn').on('click', function () {
					api.util.submitAjax({
						url: '/contents/MDC/MAIN/main/extendSession.cmd',
						success: function (data) {
							if (api.util.isErrorCode(data)) {
								confirmForLogout();
							} else {
								$('#jsLogoutTime').text(SESSION_TIMEOUT + '분 00초');
								timeoutForLogout();
							}
						}
					});
				});

				//=== GNB 메뉴... START
				// 통계메뉴에 있을 때는 대메뉴로 메뉴 이동시 화면이 새로고침 되면 안되고
				// 좌측 메뉴 트리만 바뀌어야 한다.
				var href = location.href;
				var isMdi = href.indexOf('mdiLoader') > -1 ? true : false;
        var $mnlnb2Depth = $('.CI-MDI-MENU-ALWAYS-ACTIVE','#jsMdiMenu');
				$('.jsMenuLink', '#jsGnbArea').click(function () {
					// 현재 통계 MDI 화면임
					if ( isMdi ) {
						//= 대메뉴 닫기
						$('#jsGnbArea > div').slideUp();
						//=/

						//= 트리메뉴 변경
						var $this = $(this);
						var menuIdSel = $this.attr('data-depth-menu-id');

						// 대메뉴 1 Depth 판별(length==5) 후 2 Depth 변환 (어설프지만 넘어가자;;;)
						if ( menuIdSel.length === 5 ) {
							menuIdSel = menuIdSel + '01';
						}

						$mnlnb2Depth.each(function () {
							$this = $(this);
							if ( menuIdSel ===  $this.attr('data-depth-menu-id')) { $this.css('display', ''); }
							else { $this.css('display', 'none');}
						});
						//=/

						return false;
					}

					return true;
				});
				//===/ GNB 메뉴... End

        //==== 전체메뉴: S
        // 1depth 메뉴 클릭
        $('.allmenu .allmenu_left a').on('click', function () {
          var $li = $(this).closest('li');
          $li.addClass('on').siblings().removeClass('on');
          $('.allmenu .group_wrap').hide().eq($li.index()).show();
        });

        // 2depth 메뉴 클릭
        $('.allmenu .group1 > a').on('click', function () {
          var $this = $(this);

          // 새 윈도우 링크이면 a 태그 기본 기능으로 처리
					if ($this.attr('target') === '_blank') {
						return;
					}

					var $group1 = $this.parent('div.group1');
					var $group2 = $group1.next();
					if ($group1.length === 0) return;

          var $span = $this.find('span:not(.menu-name):not(.arrow):not(.nodepth)');
          if ($span.length === 0) return;
          if ($span.hasClass('open')) { // 열려있는 상태
            $span.attr({
              class: 'close',
              title: '메뉴 닫기'
            }).text('메뉴 닫기');

						$group2.find('a').addClass('on');
						$group2.find('ul').show();

            //$this.parent('.group1').next('.group2').hide();

          } else { // 닫혀있는 상태
            $span.attr({
              class: 'open',
              title: '메뉴 펼치기'
            }).text('메뉴 펼치기');

						$group2.find('a').removeClass('on');
						$group2.find('> ul').find('ul').hide();

            //$this.parent('.group1').next('.group2').show();
          }
        });

        // 3depth 이하 메뉴 클릭
        $('.allmenu .group2 a').on('click', function () {
          var $this = $(this);
          if ($this.hasClass('nodepth')) {

          } else {
            $this.toggleClass('on');
            $this.siblings('ul').toggle();
          }
        });

        // 전체메뉴 검색 파라미터
        var menusSearchedForAllMenu = {
					word: '',
					seq: 0,
        	$menus: []
				};

        // 전체메뉴 검색 파라미터 초기화
        var resetMenusSearchedForAllMenu = function () {
					menusSearchedForAllMenu.word = '';
					menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq = 0;
					menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus.forEach(function ($menu) {
						$menu.html($menu.attr('data-menu-name'));
					});
					menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus = [];
				};

        // 전체메뉴 검색 수행
        var focusMenuSearchedForAllMenu = function () {
					if (menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus.length === 0) return;

					var $menu = menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus[menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq];
					var $prevMenu;
					if (menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq === 0) {
						$prevMenu = menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus[menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus.length - 1];
					} else {
						$prevMenu = menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus[menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq - 1];
					}

					// 검색 대상 배경색상변경
					$prevMenu.find('em').removeClass('focus');
					$menu.find('em').addClass('focus');

					// 상위 메뉴 열기
					$menu.parentsUntil('.group2', 'ul').each(function (index, ul) {
						$(ul).show().siblings('a').addClass('on');
					});
					$('.allmenu .allmenu_left li').eq($menu.closest('.group_wrap').index()).find('a').click();

					// 검색 대상 포커스
					$menu[0].scrollIntoView(false);

					menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq += 1;
					if (menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq >= menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus.length) {
						menusSearchedForAllMenu.seq = 0;
					}
				};

				// 전체메뉴 검색
        $('#CI-ALL-MENU-SEARCH').on('click', function () {
        	var word = $('#CI-ALL-MENU-SEARCH-VALUE').val().trim();
        	if (word) {
        		if (word === menusSearchedForAllMenu.word) {
							focusMenuSearchedForAllMenu();
						} else {
							resetMenusSearchedForAllMenu();
							menusSearchedForAllMenu.word = word;
							// 숫자 - 화면번호 (중간어 일치 제외)
							// 문자 - 화면명 (중간어 일치 포함)
							var pattern = isNaN(word) ? word : '^' + word;
							var regexp = new RegExp(pattern, 'g');
							var $menus = $('#CI-ALL-MENU-GROUP').find('[class="menu-name"]');
							$menus.each(function (index, menu) {
								var $menu = $(menu);
								var name = $menu.attr('data-menu-name');
								var screenNo = $menu.attr('data-screen-no');

								if (regexp.test(name) ) {
									$menu.html(name.replace(regexp, '<em>' + word + '</em>'));
									menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus.push($menu);
								}
								// 화면번호 검색은 화면명 전체 강조 표시
								else if (regexp.test(screenNo)) {
									$menu.html('<em>' + name + '</em>');
									menusSearchedForAllMenu.$menus.push($menu);
								}
							});
							focusMenuSearchedForAllMenu();
						}
					} else {
        		resetMenusSearchedForAllMenu();
					}
				});

				// 전체메뉴 검색 엔터 이벤트
        $('#CI-ALL-MENU-SEARCH-VALUE').on('keyup', function (e) {
					if (e.keyCode === 13) $('#CI-ALL-MENU-SEARCH').click();
				});

				// 전체메뉴 확대/축소
				$('.allmenu .allmenu_btn.wide').on('click', function () {
					$(this).toggleClass('on');
					$('.allmenu').toggleClass('wide');
				});

        // 전체메뉴 닫기
        $('.allmenu .allmenu_btn.close').on('click', function () {
          $('#CI-ALL-MENU-LAYER').hide();
        });

        // 전체메뉴 열기
        $('.CI-ALL-MENU-LAYER-OPEN').on('click', function () {
          $('#CI-ALL-MENU-LAYER').show();
          $('#CI-ALL-MENU-SEARCH-VALUE').focus();
        });

        // 전체목록 다운로드
				$('body').on('click', '.CI-ALL-MENU-DOWNLOAD', function () {
					var type = $(this).attr('data-type');
					var f = document.TEMPLET_FORM;
					f.action = '/contents/MDC/MAIN/main/downloadMenu.cmd?type=' + type;
					f.submit();
				});
				// 전체메뉴: E

			}
		});

		mdc.module.setModule({
			name: 'SEARCH_MODULE',
			function: function(self, api) {

				// 화면검색 하위버튼 선택
				$('#jsSchTp li').on('click', function () {
					$('#jsSchTp dt').text($(this).text());
					$('#jsSchTp dt').data('type', $(this).data('type'));
					if ($(this).data('type') === 'isu') {
						$('#jsTotSchArea > .pop_searching_txt').show();
					} else if ($(this).data('type') === 'tot') {
						$('#jsTotSchArea > .pop_searching_txt').hide();
					} else {
						$('#jsTotSchArea > .pop_searching_txt').hide();
					}
					searchEng($('#jsSchTp > dt').data('type'));
				});

				//종목검색 하위 탭 클릭
				$('#jsTotSchArea li').on('click', function () {
					$('#jsTotSchArea li').removeClass('on');
					$(this).addClass('on');
					if ($(this).data('type') === 'BND') {
						$('#jsSchRsTbl').addClass('typeBND');
					} else {
						$('#jsSchRsTbl').removeClass('typeBND');
					}
					searchEng($('#jsSchTp > dt').data('type'));
				});

				//통합검색 포커스 IN
				$('#jsTotSch').on('focus', function () {
					if ($('#jsTotSch').val() !== '' && $('#jsSchTp > dt').data('type') !== 'tot') {
						$('#jsTotSchArea').show();
						searchEng($('#jsSchTp > dt').data('type'));
					}
				});

				//통합검색 포커스 OUT
				$(document).on('click', function (e) {
					var $target = $(e.target);
					if ($('#jsTotSchArea').css('display') === 'none') return;
					if ($target.attr('class') === 'jsTotSchBlock' || $target.closest('.jsTotSchBlock').length > 0) return;
					$('#jsTotSchArea').hide();
				});

				//통합검색 키입력 & 검색 엔터 이벤트
				$('#jsTotSch').on('keyup', function () {
					var schTxt = $('#jsTotSch').val();
					var regExp = /^[ㄱ-ㅎ|가-힣|a-z|A-Z|0-9| ]+$/;
					if (!regExp.test(schTxt)) {
						for (var i = 0; i < schTxt.length; i++) {
							if (!regExp.test(schTxt[i])) {
								schTxt = schTxt.replace(schTxt[i], '');
								i--;
							}
						}
						$('#jsTotSch').val(schTxt);
					}
				}).on('keyup.search', _.debounce(function (e) {
					var schTxt = $('#jsTotSch').val();
					if (/^[ㄱ-ㅎ]+$/.test(schTxt)) {
						return false;
					}

					$('#jsTotSchArea').show();
					searchEng($('#jsSchTp > dt').data('type'));

					if (e.keyCode === 13) $('#jsTotSchBtn').click();
				}, 500));

				$('#jsTotSchBtn').on('click', function (e) {
					var url = '';
					var type = $('#jsSchTp dt').data('type');
					var keyword = $('#jsTotSch').val();
					var bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/equalSearch.cmd';
					searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, type, '', keyword, 99999, function (resp) {
						if (resp.result && resp.result.length === 1) {
							goSearchPage(resp.result[0]);
						} else {
							if (type === 'tot') {
								url = '/contents/MDC/COMS/search/MDCCOMS901.cmd?keyword='
							} else if (type === 'isu') {
								url = '/contents/MDC/COMS/search/MDCCOMS902.cmd?keyword='
							} else if (type === 'menu') {
								url = '/contents/MDC/COMS/search/MDCCOMS903.cmd?keyword='
							} else if (type === 'dict') {
								url = '/contents/MDC/COMS/search/MDCCOMS904.cmd?keyword='
							}

							url += encodeURI($('#jsTotSch').val());
							location.href = url;
						}
					});


				});

				var g_tot_idx = 1;
				var searchEng = function (type) {
					var bld = '';
					var keyword = $('#jsTotSch').val();
					$('#jsTotSchArea').find('tbody').html('');
					if (type === 'isu') {
						if ($('#jsTotSchArea li.on').data('type') === 'RECENT') {
							$('#jsSchRsTbl').html('');
							var data = getLocalStorage().searchList;
							for (var i = 0; i < data.length; i++) {
								var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
									$('<DIV>', {class: 'type01'}).append(
										$('<p>').text(data[i].isu_abbrv)
									)
								);
								item[0].stockData = data[i];
								$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
							}
							return false;
						}
						bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/isuCore.cmd';
						searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, '', $('#jsTotSchArea li.on').data('type'), keyword, 20, function (resp) {
							if (resp.result.length > 0) {
								for (var i = 0; i < resp.result.length; i++) {
									var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
										$('<DIV>', {class: 'type02'}).append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].isu_tp[0] === 'IDX' ? '지수' : resp.result[i].isu_srt_cd)
										).append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].isu_abbrv)
										).append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].mkt_nm)
										)
									);
									item[0].stockData = resp.result[i];
									$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
								}
							} else {
								$('#jsTotSchArea').find('tbody').html(
									$('<TR>').append(
										$('<TD>').append(api.lang.getMessage("MG010")) // 검색결과가 없습니다.
									)
								);
							}
						});
					} else if (type === 'menu') {
						bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/menuCore.cmd';
						searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, '', '', keyword, 20, function (resp) {
							if (resp.result.length > 0) {
								for (var i = 0; i < resp.result.length; i++) {
									var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
										$('<DIV>', {class: 'type03'}).append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].scren_no)
										).append(
											$('<SECTION>').append(
												$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].org_menu_nm)
											).append(
												$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].menu_nm)
											)
										)
									);
									item[0].stockData = resp.result[i];
									$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
								}
							} else {
								$('#jsTotSchArea').find('tbody').html(
									$('<TR>').append(
										$('<TD>').append(api.lang.getMessage("MG010")) // 검색결과가 없습니다.
									)
								);
							}
						});
					} else if (type === 'dict') {
						bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/dictCore.cmd';
						searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, '', '', keyword, 20, function (resp) {
							if (resp.result.length > 0) {
								for (var i = 0; i < resp.result.length; i++) {
									var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
										$('<DIV>', {class: 'type01'}).append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].trm_nm)
										)
									);
									item[0].stockData = resp.result[i];
									$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
								}
							} else {
								$('#jsTotSchArea').find('tbody').html(
									$('<TR>').append(
										$('<TD>').append(api.lang.getMessage("MG010")) // 검색결과가 없습니다.
									)
								);
							}

						});
					} else if (type === 'tot') {

						bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/isuCore.cmd';
						searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, '', '', keyword, 10, function (resp) {

							for (var i = 0; i < resp.result.length; i++) {
								var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
									$('<DIV>', {class: 'type02'}).append(
										$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].isu_tp[0] === 'IDX' ? '지수' : resp.result[i].isu_srt_cd)
									).append(
										$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].isu_abbrv)
									).append(
										$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].mkt_nm)
									)
								);
								item[0].stockData = resp.result[i];
								$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
							}
						});

						bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/menuCore.cmd';
						searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, '', '', keyword, 10, function (resp) {
							for (var i = 0; i < resp.result.length; i++) {
								var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
									$('<DIV>', {class: 'type03'}).append(
										$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].scren_no)
									).append(
										$('<SECTION>').append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].org_menu_nm)
										).append(
											$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].menu_nm)
										)
									)
								);
								item[0].stockData = resp.result[i];
								$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
							}
						});


						bld = '/comm/util/SearchEngine/dictCore.cmd';
						searchResult.init($('#jsTotSchArea'), bld, '', '', keyword, 10, function (resp) {
							for (var i = 0; i < resp.result.length; i++) {
								var item = $('<A>', {href: '#', class: 'CI-STOCK-SEARCH-RECENT-WORD'}).append(
									$('<DIV>', {class: 'type01'}).append(
										$('<p>').text(resp.result[i].trm_nm)
									)
								);
								item[0].stockData = resp.result[i];
								$('#jsSchRsTbl').append($('<TR>').append($('<TD>').append(item)));
							}
						});

					}

				};

				var searchResult = {};
				searchResult.init = function ($obj, bld, type, solrIsuType, solrKeyword, s_pagenum, callback) {
					var result;
					var PAGENUM = 100;
					if (s_pagenum) PAGENUM = s_pagenum;

					function getList() {
						api.util.submitAjax({
							url: bld + "?isAutoCom=true&type=" + type + '&solrIsuType=' + encodeURI(solrIsuType) + '&solrKeyword=' + encodeURI(solrKeyword) + '&rows=' + PAGENUM + '&start=0',
							useFetch: true,
							async: false,
							success: function (resp) {
								if (resp.result.length === 0) {
									api.util.submitAjax({
										url: bld + "?isAutoCom=true&type=" + type + '&solrIsuType=' + encodeURI(solrIsuType) + '&solrKeyword=' + encodeURI(AtoH.convert(solrKeyword)) + '&rows=' + PAGENUM + '&start=0',
										useFetch: true,
										async: false,
										success: function (resp) {
											if (resp.result.length === 0) {
												result = resp;
												appendData();
											} else {
												result = resp;
												appendData();
											}
										}
									});
								} else {
									result = resp;

									appendData();
								}
							}
						});
					}

					function appendData() {
						if (typeof callback === 'function') callback(result);
					}

					getList();

					return {
						getList: getList,
						getResult: function () {
							return result;
						}
					};
				};

				var getLocalStorage = function () {
					return api.util.getLocalStorage('krx_mdc.total_search');
				};

				var setLocalStorage = function (storage) {
					api.util.setLocalStorage('krx_mdc.total_search', storage);
				};

				var saveItemToLocalStorage = function (item) {
					var storage = getLocalStorage();
					storage.searchList = storage.searchList.filter(function (data) {
						if (data['isu_cd'][0] !== item['isu_cd'][0]) return true;
					});
					storage.searchList.unshift(item);
					storage.searchWord = storage.searchWord.filter(function (data) {
						if (data['isu_cd'][0] !== item['isu_cd'][0]) return true;
					});
					storage.searchWord.unshift(item);
					if (storage.searchList.length > 20) storage.searchList.pop();
					if (storage.searchWord.length > 10) storage.searchWord.pop();
					setLocalStorage(storage);
				};

				$('#jsSchRsTbl').on('click', 'a', function () {
					var item = $(this)[0].stockData;
					goSearchPage(item);
				});

				var goSearchPage = function (item) {
					var cookieId = '';
					var typeNo = '';
					var link = '';

					/************************ 메뉴 ****************************/
					if (item.scren_url !== undefined) {
						var menu_nm = item.menu_nm[0];
						var menu_id = item.menu_id[0];
						var scren_url = item.scren_url[0];

						if (menu_nm.indexOf('통계 > 기본 통계') !== -1 || menu_nm.indexOf('통계 > 이슈 통계') !== -1 || menu_nm.indexOf('통계 > 공매도 통계') !== -1
							|| menu_nm.indexOf('통계 > 통계DB 정보') !== -1 || menu_nm.indexOf('쉽게 보는 통계 > 주요 통계') !== -1 || menu_nm.indexOf('쉽게 보는 통계 > 순위 통계') !== -1
							|| menu_nm.indexOf('쉽게 보는 통계 > TR통계') !== -1) {
							location.href = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=' + encodeURI(menu_id);
						} else {
							location.href = scren_url;
						}
					}
					/************************ 메뉴 ****************************/

					/************************ 종목 ****************************/
					if (item.isu_tp !== undefined) {
						if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'STK') { //주식 STK
							cookieId = 'finder_stkisu';
							link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201020203';
						} else if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'BND') { //채권 BND - KTS / BND / SMB
							cookieId = 'finder_bondisu';
							link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201040202';
						} else if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'SECU') { //증권상품 SECU - EF / EN / EW
							cookieId = 'finder_secuprodisu';
							if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'EF') {
								typeNo = '1';
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201030105';
							} else if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'EN') {
								typeNo = '2';
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201030205';
							} else if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'EW') {
								typeNo = '3';
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201030304';
							}
						} else if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'DRV') { //파생상품 DRV - FU / OP
							cookieId = 'finder_drvprodisu';
							link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201050202';
						} else if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'GEN') { //일반상품 GEN - CMD / ETS / OIL
							cookieId = '';
							if (item.mkt_id[0] === 'CMD') {
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201060204';
							} else if (item.mkt_id[0] === 'ETS') {
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201060304';
							} else if (item.mkt_id[0] === 'OIL') {
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201060102';
							}
						} else if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'IDX') { //지수 IDX
							cookieId = '';
							if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'STK_IDX') {
								cookieId = 'finder_equidx';
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201010105';
							} else if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'DRV_ETC') {
								cookieId = 'finder_drvetcidx';
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201010305';
							} else if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'BND_IDX') {
								cookieId = '';
								link = '/contents/MDC/MDI/mdiLoader/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0201010202';
							}
						}

						if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'IDX') {
							if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'STK_IDX' || item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'DRV_ETC') {
								if (cookieId !== '') {
									var input = {
										lang: 'ko_KR',
										finderCd: cookieId,
										tbox: item['isu_abbrv'],
										codeNm: item['isu_abbrv'],
										codeVal: item['isu_cd'][0],
										codeVal2: item['isu_srt_cd'][0],
										typeNo: typeNo,
										param1: item['mkt_id']
									};

									mdc.util.setFinderStorage(input);
									saveItemToLocalStorage(item);
								}
							} else if (item.isu_tp_dtl[0] === 'BND_IDX') {
								if (item['isu_cd'][0] === '100000000') {
									link = link + '&p_indTp=1';
								} else if (item['isu_cd'][0] === 'KTB') {
									link = link + '&p_indTp=3';
								} else if (item['isu_cd'][0] === '200010000') {
									link = link + '&p_indTp=2';
								}
								saveItemToLocalStorage(item);
							}
						} else {
							if (cookieId !== '') {
								var input = {
									lang: 'ko_KR',
									finderCd: cookieId,
									tbox: item['isu_srt_cd'][0] + '/' + item['isu_abbrv'],
									codeNm: item['isu_abbrv'],
									codeVal: item['isu_cd'][0],
									codeVal2: '',
									typeNo: typeNo,
									param1: ''
								};

								if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'DRV') {
									input.codeVal2 = item['prod_id'][0];
								} else {
									input.codeVal2 = item['isu_cd'][0];
								}

								if (item.isu_tp[0] === 'BND') { //채권 BND - KTS / BND / SMB
									if (item.mkt_id[0] === 'KTS') {
										input.param1 = '1';
									} else if (item.mkt_id[0] === 'BND') {
										input.param1 = '2';
									} else if (item.mkt_id[0] === 'SMB') {
										input.param1 = '6';
									}
								}
								mdc.util.setFinderStorage(input);
								saveItemToLocalStorage(item);
							}
						}

						if(link !== ''){
							location.href = link;
						}
					};
					/************************ 종목 ****************************/

					/************************ 용어 ****************************/
					if (item.trm_nm !== undefined) {
						window.open('/contents/MDC/STAT/dataDic/dictionary/index.cmd?menuId=MDC0205&schTxt=' + encodeURI(item.trm_nm), 'MDC0205', 'width=1000,height=800,resizable=yes');
					}
					/************************ 용어 ****************************/

				}
			}
		});
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
